# Tasks With Mixed `phase_captions` Structure

Source CSV: `data/juno_zion_tasks_export_2026-05-14_to_2026-05-14.csv`

This document lists tasks where `phase_captions` contains both the standard structure and the alternate structure.

Standard structure uses `caption` and/or `phase_index`.
Alternate structure uses `description`, `idx`, and/or `hand`.

## Summary

- Mixed tasks found: `121`
- Alternate structure only on the last phase: `107`
- Alternate structure on the last phase and earlier phases: `14`
